# ButtonStyle[¶](https://docs.aiogram.dev/en/latest/api/enums/button_style.html#module-aiogram.enums.button_style)

[¶](https://docs.aiogram.dev/en/latest/api/enums/button_style.html#module-aiogram.enums.button_style)
[[source]](https://docs.aiogram.dev/en/latest/_modules/aiogram/enums/button_style.html#ButtonStyle)
[¶](https://docs.aiogram.dev/en/latest/api/enums/button_style.html#aiogram.enums.button_style.ButtonStyle)
This object represents a button style (inline- or reply-keyboard).
